Important News

The Central Party Department and the National Government's Memorial Week 69

The Central Party Department held the 50th Dr. Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week in the auditorium at 9:00 AM on the 10th. 500 people attended including central committee members, staff of various departments and commissions, and guests. Ye Chucang chaired the meeting. After the ceremony, the chairman reported, saying, "Recently, there have been two important events in the Party. One is the completion of the Third Plenary Session, and the other is that the Yan Xishan issue has come to an end. Since Yan issued his telegram, the public generally believed that his reasons were untenable. He also realized his mistake. Party comrades, under serious circumstances, were able to demonstrate justice, preventing all reactionaries from succeeding in their ambition to betray the Central Government and from deceiving the people with inexplicable fallacies. During this period, we have indeed been tested. The armed comrades listed in Yan's telegram, except for a few notoriously rebellious elements, have recently telegraphed to deny this, requesting the Central Government to use force to punish Yan, and are willing to be the vanguard in the punitive expedition. Party comrades at home and abroad have telegraphed to request the punitive expedition and are willing to be the rear guard, which is countless. Comrades in Peiping, Tianjin, and Shanxi, despite being subjected to heavy pressure, were able to work hard with a fearless spirit, and finally regained their freedom and completed their mission. This shows that the Party's doctrine has given the people a deep understanding, and all comrades can use the correct concept to distinguish between right and wrong, on the one hand expressing the claim of unyielding, on the other hand, carrying forward the spirit of peaceful reunification, so that the Party can achieve the final victory, which is the most comforting and most gratifying thing. On the central side, there were available troops, but they were not used out of love for peace. On the reactionary side, although there were no available troops, they wanted to use them for betrayal. The facts have been obvious. Those with simple minds want to repeat the old tricks of warlords, thinking that the method of scaring Li Yuanhong and Xu Shichang with a piece of telegram can be used again. This is due to a lack of understanding of the revolutionary spirit and the meaning of the revolution. Revolutionary comrades are never scared or deceived. The more intense the reaction, the greater the spirit of the Party. At this time when the situation is about to be resolved, a few people observe that it is the resolution of the central government's problems with the Northwest and the problems between Chiang and Yan, which is a mistake. In an independent and unified country, there must not be an object to stand against it. In the organization of a country, there cannot be a central government. There cannot be a representative in the government. For example, in a school, students of all levels should be led by the principal. The principal exercises leadership duties in a proper capacity, not managing the school in a personal capacity, which cannot be called running the school single-handedly. For example, newly appointed ambassadors to China must present their credentials to the National Government, and must present them to the representative of the Republic of China, and must not be respected in a personal capacity or any other force. This is clear. Chairman Chiang is the Marshal of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, entrusted by the Republic of China, and controls the national military with the entire central name, commanding the national army. His response to all reactions is by no means a problem between someone and someone. If this point cannot be understood thoroughly, then right and wrong, merits and demerits, cannot be judged, and the future of the country will be even more hopeless." After the report, the meeting adjourned.

The National Government held the Dr. Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week at 10:00 AM on the same day. Chiang Kai-shek, Tan Yankai, Hu Hanmin, Gu Yingfen, He Yingqin, He Yaozu, Chen Shaokuan, Chen Yi, Yi Peiji, Liu Jiwen, and more than 300 officials from the National Government's Civil Affairs and Military Affairs departments attended. Chiang Kai-shek chaired the meeting. After the ceremony, Qian Changzhao, Secretary of the National Government, gave a political report, followed by a speech by Chiang, urging officials of various departments to implement the resolutions of the Third Plenary Session. The meeting adjourned. The report and speech are recorded separately below.

Qian Changzhao reported that the Third Plenary Session closed last Thursday. Many resolutions were made at this plenary session. On the positive side, such as local self-government, economic construction, and popular education, most of the implementation methods and steps have been decided. On the negative side, such as eliminating bandits, etc., the implementation methods and steps have also been decided. From now on, the Party Department and the government can implement them practically. Regarding local self-government, we know that this kind of work is the foundation of other works during the tutelage period. Only when local self-government is successful can social undertakings be fully developed. However, local self-government focuses on the county, and there are two very important points in the conduct of party affairs and politics in each county. One is to have a sound Party Department and a competent and ethical magistrate, and the other is to have everyone understand the boundaries between the Party Department and the government, so as to ensure that there are no disputes and conflicts between the Party and the government. These two points have been taken into account in the plenary session. Regarding economic construction, there are now many constructions, which are difficult to carry out at the same time. Therefore, among various undertakings, we must distinguish between urgency and priority, and even in one undertaking, the work of each part must be distinguished between urgency and priority. When our country's human and financial resources are very scarce and very difficult, the most taboo is to support empty shows. At this moment, let me give an example. The so-called construction in Shanxi before the eleventh year of the Republic of China (let alone after the eleventh year) committed the problem of supporting empty shows. Without any preparation of human and financial resources, many agencies were set up. It looks as if everything is being done, but in fact, nothing is done or there is nothing to do. However, a few signs are hung up. The failure of Shanxi is a small example, and if the whole country engages in construction undertakings in this uneconomical way, it will surely fail. The tutelage period is very short, and we should work down-to-earth. All plans must be carefully considered, and we must not try them lightly. This point was also discussed in detail at the plenary session, and the construction from now on will be carried out in accordance with the needs of the people, based on human and financial resources, and in sequence. Regarding education, its importance is known to all. The plenary session declaration also stated that "from now on, our efforts must not only build a society of the Three Principles of the People through education but also enrich the country of the Three Principles of the People through education." I think there is one thing that brooks no delay, which is the determination of education funding. A clever woman cannot cook without rice. If there is no definite funding, education cannot be done well. Just look at the capital special municipality, with a population of more than 500,000 and more than 50,000 school-age children, but the city's elementary school funding is only more than 30,000 yuan per month. There are 34 elementary schools, with more than 11,000 students. As a result, there are more than 700 private schools, with more than 18,000 students. Because of funding, the City Education Bureau cannot add elementary schools or classrooms. Recently, there have been more than 3,000 children who have registered but cannot be admitted. Even parents and brothers surround the school and ask why their children are not allowed to enroll. This phenomenon is extremely pitiful. If the capital is like this,

Page 9

News Highlights 70

This is the case everywhere else. It is the case in elementary schools, middle schools, and universities alike. There is indeed a pressing need to seek remedies. The education funds for each province, city, and county nationwide should be earnestly determined. The above is the focus on the positive aspects of the Third Plenary Session. The elimination of bandits, from a negative perspective, is comparatively more important. Currently, bandits are everywhere, and the general populace cannot live and work in peace. Some are dead, others are displaced. Some people with assets dare not live in the countryside, and some even dare not live in small towns. As a result, the countryside becomes poorer and poorer every day, turning into a world of thieves. If this continues, the vitality of the people will be almost exhausted, and future recovery will be extremely difficult. The Plenary Session specifically put forward a special project for this reason. In any case, bandits must be eradicated in the shortest possible time. Orders must be carried out, otherwise all social undertakings will be impossible to carry out. In short, the significance of this meeting is very great. All the resolutions are suitable for China's current needs. As long as we earnestly work hard, the implementation of political tutelage will definitely be very smooth. Mr. Yan Xishan telegraphed his resignation. Mr. Zhao Daiwen telegraphed, mentioning that Mr. Yan had a great awakening and was willing to go abroad. Mr. Yan's remarks before his resignation were like a bolt from the blue, while this resignation was like the sudden clearing of the clouds to reveal the sun when a storm is about to break. It may not be a blessing for the Party and the country. What Mr. Zhao meant by Mr. Yan's great awakening must have been partly a feeling that his previous words and deeds towards the Central Government were not loyal to the Party, and partly a regret for falling into the trap of the reactionaries. If Mr. Yan has truly awakened, his resignation is natural, and his willingness to go abroad is also a very smart move. Because the general public, after several civil wars, are like birds startled by the twang of a bow. They see Mr. Yan's bizarre attitude, and if there is no action now to show his sincerity, their suspicions and fears will still exist. Mr. Yan's departure abroad can somewhat show his sincerity, and society can be stabilized. Moreover, the reactionaries are ubiquitous. Even if Mr. Yan has a great awakening, they will still try to maintain ties with him, and may even go to surround him. Since the bad environment cannot be changed immediately, it is better to leave, so that both body and mind can find peace. Therefore, for the sake of the Party and the country, and for the sake of Mr. Yan's personal interests, going abroad is the best policy. As for the Central Government, it has always been broad-minded. As long as peace and unification are achieved, it will still try to help Mr. Yan in any way that does not compromise the overall situation and can enhance his personal reputation. Chairman Chiang's speech: The Third Plenary Session has concluded. It has been found that at the Second Plenary Session, many important cases were resolved. By the time the Third Plenary Session was convened, the audit of what had been implemented in accordance with the resolutions in the past eight months was only about one-tenth or two-tenths of what was decided. This was because the various departments below the government failed to pay attention, and this phenomenon occurred. Although the Party headquarters and the government repeatedly urged at that time, some departments simply ignored it. The Chinese people's problem is that they can talk but cannot act. Foreigners have also criticized our country for this. In the future, it is hoped that the various departments will pay close attention to the various resolutions of the Third Plenary Session and the declarations of the Congress, and strive to realize them, so as to avoid criticism from foreigners. In addition, during the revolutionary era, Party and government colleagues were concerned about relying on personal conscience and working hard. For this resolution, do not use the excuse of lack of economic resources and talent, and strive to do it. Also, regarding the issue of thrift and reducing government spending, the various departments must improve at any time. The chief officer in charge must conduct on-site inspections of the department members, and must use their mouths, eyes, hands, and hearts. Do not be greedy and insatiable. Redundant personnel must be reduced, so that useful funds can be freed up to engage in construction.

Ministry of Finance's Financial Report for the 17th Year 71

(Continued) (Continued)

Although the government has been facing military affairs and has been busy in recent years with domestic and foreign debts without collateral, in order to maintain national credit, it has appointed the President of the Executive Yuan, the Minister of Finance, and relevant ministers and important personnel to form a special committee to study and discuss the plan for repaying domestic and foreign debts without collateral. As a result, significant progress has been made. This year, a definite method can be determined. The initial plan is for the government to allocate 5 million yuan annually as preparation for clearing the case.

Someone in the country once suggested that if the Ministry of Finance wants to obtain economic assistance, it should find ways to borrow foreign debt. However, the policy of the Ministry of Finance is that foreign debt can only be accepted if the conditions are appropriate and do not harm the country's economic sovereignty. Otherwise, it will never be contacted. In the past year, the Ministry of Finance has comprehensively planned the debts for which the ministry is responsible for the domestic and foreign debt issues, and formulated a proper repayment plan, so that one party will not harm national rights, and the other party will be satisfied with the general creditors.

At the same time, the Ministry of Finance earnestly hopes that the various government agencies will give full understanding and recognition. It takes a lot of effort to restore national credit, and it is not easy. It relies on the strength of the group. In particular, it is hoped that no matter where, do not regard rash borrowing as a trivial matter. It is important to know that partial default of the government is enough to affect the whole, and the credibility of all countries to us will also have considerable losses. In other words, the country's credit is closely related to the government as a whole, and a slight movement can affect the whole body.

Government bonds and treasury bills: In recent years, the government has had to issue government bonds and treasury bills again and again in order to unify the military and implement demobilization. However, things went against expectations, and the purpose of demobilization was difficult to achieve. However, the issued bonds are guaranteed by extremely reliable income, and at the same time, representatives of various banks and groups are ordered to convene to form a fund custody committee. Therefore, the bonds have become a major market. In addition to banks, ordinary people are also very enthusiastic about buying and selling bonds. On the one hand, it is due to the stagnant business and surplus funds. On the other hand, it can also prove the value of government bonds, which is enough to make the general public believe in them.

Issuing bonds for a long time to meet the urgent needs of the military and political affairs is indeed an expedient measure, and it is by no means the right way to manage finances. The financial authorities know this best. However, because peace has not been restored, a comprehensive policy cannot be implemented. In order to cope with the current environment, this is a last resort. The fundamental solution is still to achieve peace before it is possible to reorganize.

Central Bank: Our party successively established the Central Bank in Guangzhou and Hankou, and experienced hardships. However, it was not discouraged by this, and the policy of organizing this bank has never been changed. However, before the Northern Expedition was successful, if paper money was issued indiscriminately to fill the military needs, the future financial risks would be unimaginable. Therefore, the establishment of the Central Bank was delayed. It was not until the completion of the Northern Expedition that it was established on November 1, 17th year. At the same time, the Ministry of Finance formulated regulations and systems, and the management of business was particularly strict. The handling of paper money was particularly cautious, and the government and various public groups, the board of directors and the board of supervisors, worked together to handle the bank's affairs, in order to show great trust. Therefore, after more than a year of establishment, although it has repeatedly experienced various shocks in politics and military affairs, it has been able to pass through smoothly. The development in the past year is not without its spectacle. If the situation is peaceful, its future is difficult to limit.

After the establishment of the Central Bank, everything is held with prudence, and the government's financial credit is also implicitly increased. Moreover, whenever the situation is tense and interest rates soar, it uses police funds to lend to peers at lower interest rates, and the market is calm.

The domestic debt fund, which was previously deposited in foreign banks, has now been deposited in the Central Bank. If the overall situation is stable and the government's major plans are implemented, the Central Bank, due to its position, can be the central agency for reorganizing finance and maintaining the market. The asset and liability summary table of the bank one year after its establishment is attached below. (Attachment omitted)

Expert Committee: In the past two years, the Ministry of Finance has hired a number of expert committee members to plan financial improvements. In the summer of the 17th year, an economic conference was convened to solicit the opinions of bankers and businessmen across the country on economic construction. Salt affairs and tobacco and alcohol have also been assigned committee members to hold meetings to study improvements. The most important thing is the Design Committee. The committee is organized by American economic and financial experts hired by the Ministry of Finance. The chairman is Dr. Kemmerer. Dr. Kemmerer has extensive knowledge and experience. The committee's responsibility is to study major domestic currency and financial plans, such as improving the monetary system, reorganizing tax revenue, and national revenue and expenditure budgets, accounting management, and methods for restoring national credit. The results obtained have been compiled into various reports, ready to be submitted to the State Council. Among them, there are issues related to people's livelihood and national economy, which the public should pay attention to. In the future, it is also planned to publish and disseminate them. Dr. Kemmerer has completed his mission and has returned to his country. However, there are still several expert committee members who are continuing to be hired to help gather ideas.

Civil Service Examination System: The Ministry of Finance uses personnel in the same way as other government agencies. Due to the relationship between facts and needs during the Northern Expedition military era, there was no time to choose. However, there are not many talents with administrative experience. Now that the Examination Yuan has been established, there should be a perfect method to improve the system of registration and advancement.

The civil service examination system has not yet been implemented, but the Ministry of Finance still maintains the original examination procedures of the various agencies under its jurisdiction. For example, customs service personnel must pass an examination. This good system is worth maintaining. Because there is this system and order, the current method is not only for customs, but also for inland regular customs such as Wuhu Yangyou Fengyang, etc., which are now merged into the customs for handling, in order to imitate this system.

The Salt Affairs Audit Office also adopts the same policy. The most important reason for the Ministry of Finance to restore the audit offices in various places is that the office has an excellent examination system. The personnel in the office are experienced and trained. The Tobacco Tax Office under the Ministry of Finance is the third most important. Although the examination system is not fully applicable, the appointment, removal, and promotion of some personnel have also imitated the examination system. In the future, the candidates for the director of the office may change, but the staff can definitely not be changed in conjunction.

The annual amount of Likin revenue is as high as 70 million yuan. Although it is nominally a national tax, the personnel who handle it are dispatched by the local authorities. There are numerous bureaus and cards. The collection method is extremely cumbersome, and the personnel are extremely mixed. There are hundreds of malpractices, which is inevitable. This kind of agency has no fundamental improvement method. Even if there is a good examination system, it will not help. The only thing is to resolutely abolish it at the scheduled time.

After the abolition of Likin, customs, salt, and cigarette tax revenue accounts for nine-tenths of the ministry's revenue. Since the examination system has been adopted for most of it, it should not be difficult for all agencies under the Ministry of Finance to adopt the examination system in the future. However, the salaries of customs and audit personnel are relatively high compared to other agencies, so the issue of treatment standards is slightly difficult.

Cultivating the integrity of the general staff and a good atmosphere cannot be achieved without strictly implementing the examination system and guaranteeing the law. This system is the only fundamental way to solve the problem of personnel.

Budget: Although there are military bandits and famines in the country, the price of silver has fallen, and there is financial panic, the financial problem is not absolutely impossible to solve. It is only when the situation is slightly peaceful, the budget can be established, the use will not be as scattered and unfounded as before, and the administration will not be as hurried as before, then the financial future can be hoped for.

Our party recognized the need for a budget early on. With the establishment of a budget, the government's work can have a certain scope and steps. Public budget can also gain the belief of the general public. Therefore, it advocates the establishment of a budget in the shortest possible time. When the Ministry of Finance holds the plenary session of the Central Executive Committee, and when it holds economic conferences, financial conferences, disarmament conferences, and demobilization conferences, it also asks the government to pay special attention to the implementation of this issue. Because the government has no budget, it will inevitably come and go from the east to the west, and support itself from the left and the right. A thorough financial plan cannot be implemented. The government only has the power to levy taxes, but has no public report on revenue and expenditure, which is a major obstacle to cooperation between the government and the people.

The biggest difficulty in establishing a budget is the inability to predict the need for and restriction of military spending. The government has also repeatedly tried its best to reduce military spending to the minimum. For example, at the first demobilization conference in February of the 18th year, the major generals of all parties saw the government's revenue and expenditure summary table, and unanimously decided that the military budget, in addition to the demobilization expenses, should be limited to 19.2 million yuan per year. However, the Guifeng warlords successively initiated turmoil, and the resolution was in vain. When Guifeng was gradually resolved, the government renewed the demobilization conference with the opportunity of reorganization, and slightly increased the military spending, setting it at 21.6 million yuan per year, plus 30 million yuan for demobilization expenses. However, the civil strife frequently occurred again in a short period of time, which forced the government to use all means to raise military supplies and overcome the difficult hurdle of borrowing from the east to the west.

The military spending listed in the table, from July of the 17th year to June of the 18th year, totaled 209,536,969 yuan. However, this number is not the total amount of military spending in the country. All expenditures in the three northeastern provinces, Rehe, Chahar, Suiyuan, Xikang, Gansu, Shanxi, Sichuan, Yunnan, Guizhou, Guangdong, and Guangxi are not included. (The military spending in the above provinces sometimes illegally forces loans, pre-levies money, grain, and donations, and uses them to cope with it.) If the total number of these provinces is combined, it exceeds the number set by the two demobilization conferences, and I don't know how many.

In the end, how should our country's military spending be limited, so that the Ministry of Finance will not have to dig everywhere, and how can the Ministry of Finance have surplus funds to take care of construction projects and repay domestic and foreign debts? The key to this is the issue of national peace. The Ministry of Finance itself cannot do anything. If this problem can be solved satisfactorily, then the future implementation of constitutional government, economic construction, international status, and financial reorganization can be easily solved. It is only through the sincere cooperation of the party, the country, and the people, and overcoming difficulties together, that success can be achieved. (End)

Regulations on the Telecommunications Government Bonds of the Ministry of Communications 72

Amended and Passed by the 79th Meeting of the Legislative Yuan

The Legislative Yuan, at its 79th meeting the day before yesterday (8th), passed the Regulations on the Telecommunications Government Bonds of the Ministry of Communications for the 19th year of the Republic of China. The full text is as follows: (Article 1) In order to reorganize and expand telegraph, telephone, and wireless communications, the Ministry of Communications specifically issues government bonds, named the Telecommunications Government Bonds of the Ministry of Communications for the 19th year of the Republic of China. (Article 2) The fixed amount of these government bonds is 10 million national currency. (Article 3) The annual interest rate of these government bonds is set at 8%. (Article 4) These government bonds will be issued on April 1, 19th year of the Republic of China. (Article 5) These government bonds will be issued at 98% of the face value. (Article 6) All international telegraph fee income of the Ministry of Communications shall be used as the principal and interest repayment fund for these government bonds. If it is insufficient, the ministry shall allocate funds from other telecommunications revenue to make up for it, and allocate it in installments to the bank designated by the fund custody committee in accordance with the principal and interest repayment schedule, and store it in a special account for payment of principal and interest due. (Article 7) The members of the fund custody committee in the preceding article shall be seven, and shall be organized by two members dispatched by the Ministry of Communications, one by the Ministry of Finance, one by the Ministry of Audit, two by the Bankers Association, and one by the Money Industry Association. The rules for the custody fund shall be separately stipulated. (Article 8) Interest on these government bonds shall be paid every six months, with the interest payment periods being September 30 and March 31 each year. (Article 9) These government bonds shall be repaid in full in ten years, from the 20th year of the Republic of China to the 29th year of the Republic of China. 1 million yuan of principal shall be repaid by lottery each year. The repayment of the principal in the preceding paragraph shall begin on March 31 each year. The lottery date shall be March 15 each year, and shall be supervised and executed by special commissioners dispatched by the Ministry of Communications and one member each dispatched by the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Audit, and the Bankers Association. (Article 10) The bonds of these government bonds are divided into five types: 10,000 yuan, 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, 10 yuan, and 5 yuan, all of which are in bearer form. (Article 11) The bonds of these government bonds may be freely bought and sold and mortgaged. When it is necessary to pay a security deposit for official business, it may be used as collateral, and may also be used as the guarantee reserve of the bank. (Article 12) Those who forge or damage the credit of the bonds of these government bonds shall be punished by the judicial authorities in accordance with the law. (Article 13) The detailed rules for the issuance of these government bonds shall be separately stipulated. (Article 14) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Labor-Capital Dispute Resolution Law Passed by the Legislative Yuan 73

(Continued)

Chapter 3 Dispute Resolution Procedures Section 1 Mediation Procedures (Article 19) When a party to a dispute applies for mediation, he/she shall submit a mediation application to the competent administrative authority. (Article 20) The mediation application shall state the following items: (1) The name, occupation, and address of the parties, or the name and factory number of the business. If it is a group, its name and location of the office. (2) The number of workers related to the dispute. (3) The main points of the dispute. (Article 21) When the competent administrative authority submits to mediation without the application of the parties to the dispute, the administrative authority shall notify the parties in writing of the matters to be mediated. (Article 22) The Mediation Committee shall begin to investigate the following matters within two days after convening: (1) The content of the dispute. (2) The written statements and other related events submitted by the parties to the dispute. (3) The current situation of both parties to the dispute. (4) Other matters to be investigated. The investigation period shall not exceed seven days unless there are special circumstances. (Article 23) The Mediation Committee may summon witnesses, order relevant persons to attend the meeting to explain, or submit written statements for the purpose of investigation. (Article 24) The Mediation Committee may investigate or inquire from relevant factories, stores, etc. (Article 25) The members of the Mediation Committee shall not disclose the confidential matters obtained from the investigation. After the investigation is completed by the Mediation Committee, it shall make a decision on mediation within two days, unless there are special circumstances or both parties to the dispute agree to extend the period. (Article 26) The mediation of the Mediation Committee shall be extended with the consent of both parties to the dispute. (Article 27) If the mediation of the Mediation Committee is agreed by the representatives of both parties to the dispute and signed in the mediation record, the mediation is established. The Mediation Committee shall report the results of the mediation to the competent administrative authority (Section 2) Arbitration Procedures (Article 28) When a party to a dispute applies for arbitration, he/she shall submit an arbitration application to the competent administrative authority. After receiving the aforementioned documents, the competent administrative authority shall convene an arbitration committee as soon as possible at the location of the administrative authority or the location of the dispute. (Article 29) When the parties to a dispute apply for arbitration because the mediation fails, their application shall state the following items: (1) The name, occupation, and address of the parties, or the name and factory number of the business. If it is a group, its name and location of the office. (2) The reason why the mediation failed. (3) The purpose of the request. (Article 30) The provisions of Articles 11 to 26 shall apply mutatis mutandis to the arbitration procedure. (Article 31) The arbitration of the arbitration committee shall be carried out by the consensus of all members, and the decision shall be made by the majority. The arbitration committee shall make an arbitration award within days and send it to both parties, and send it to the competent administrative authority for record. (Article 32) The parties to a dispute may reach a settlement regardless of the extent of the arbitration procedure, but the settlement conditions shall be reported to the arbitration committee.

Chapter 4 Restrictions on the Conduct of Parties to a Dispute (Article 33) During the mediation and arbitration period, the employer shall not suspend business or dismiss workers, and the workers shall not strike. (Article 34) Workers or workers' groups shall not have the following behaviors: (1) Closing stores or factories. (2) Taking or damaging the goods and equipment of stores and factories without authorization. (3) Forcing others to strike. Chapter 5 Penalties (Article 35) When the parties to a dispute violate the provisions of Articles 33 and 34, the competent administrative authority and the mediation committee or arbitration committee may stop them at any time. Those who refuse to obey the stop may be fined up to 200 yuan. If the behavior has violated the criminal law, it shall still be punished in accordance with the criminal law. (Article 36) One of the following behaviors shall be fined up to 100 yuan: (1) Violating the provisions of Article 23, failing to attend the meeting without reason, or failing to submit a written statement. (2) Violating the provisions of Article 25. In the case of the second item in the preceding paragraph, if it constitutes a criminal act under the criminal law, it shall still be punished in accordance with the criminal law. (Article 37) One of the following behaviors shall be fined up to 100 yuan, but if the witness makes a false statement, he/she shall be punished in accordance with the provisions of perjury in the criminal law: (1) Making a false statement in the circumstances specified in Article 23. (2) Refusing to investigate, answer, or making a false statement without reason in the circumstances specified in Article 24. (Article 38) When there is a behavior that should be punished under the provisions of each article of this chapter, the competent administrative authority and the mediation committee or arbitration committee may state the reasons and transfer the case to the competent court for trial. The court shall pronounce a judgment within 20 days after receiving the case file, unless there are special circumstances.

Chapter 6 Supplementary Provisions (Article 39) The provincial government or the municipal government not under the province may formulate detailed rules for the implementation of this law when necessary, and submit them to the National Government for approval. (Article 40) This law shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

National Meteorological Conference to Open 74

Convened by the Central Meteorological Research Institute

To be Held in Nanjing on April 16

The Meteorological Research Institute of the National Central Research Institute, in view of the increasing number of meteorological institutions in our country recently, while weather reports are still lacking in coordination, has decided to convene a national meteorological conference on April 16 of this year, gathering various institutions related to meteorological undertakings, to discuss important matters such as codes and signals, in order to achieve unified effectiveness. Letters have recently been sent to various institutions to discuss the original letter as follows: "Dear Sir, in recent years, our country's meteorological undertakings have gradually shown signs of booming, and the number of weather observation institutions is increasing day by day. However, observation and verification rely on cooperation, and the language and signals are especially important for unification. For example, meteorological codes, transmission reports, etc., all need to be standardized. Our institute has now approved the letter from the Meteorological Society of China, requesting to notify all weather observation institutions and various associations related to meteorology across the country to hold a national meteorological conference on a regular basis to consolidate and so on. It is very necessary. It is now scheduled to be held at the Meteorological Research Institute of the Arctic Pavilion in the capital on April 16 of this year. The National Meteorological Conference will discuss meteorological codes, observation time, transmission methods, meteorological signals, etc., in order to seek unity. Please prepare proposals and send representatives to attend the meeting accordingly. Please check and handle it. Please also reply if you can send representatives to attend at that time. I sincerely appreciate your friendship."

Jin Army Withdraws North and Tianjin-Pukou Railway Traffic 75

Jinan Correspondence: This time, the provincial army's withdrawal from Dezhou and the Jin army's advance into Dezhou are actions to avoid conflict. In fact, there is no war. Now that the situation has eased, it is not difficult to resolve it with political means. The Tianjin-Pukou Railway runs through the north and south. Since the railway bridge over the Yellow River Cliff in northern Shandong was destroyed, traffic has been interrupted for a week, and goods have been piled up, and travelers have sighed. Everyone is eager for traffic to resume as soon as possible. According to news received today, Fu Zuoyi has telegraphed, stating that the troops under his command will never cross the northern border of Hebei, and asked to repair the bridge and resume traffic as soon as possible. It is said that Chen Tiaoyuan is currently discussing with the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Bureau, and the date of resumption of traffic may not be far away. As for the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Yellow River Iron Bridge, which was blown up on the evening of the 2nd, the section in Jinjin should be repaired by Tianjin, but due to the interruption of the railway, Tianjin cannot come south. Therefore, the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Bureau telegraphed the Jinan-Han section to survey and repair in order to restore traffic. Engineer Hu Shenghong has followed the order to go to Jinbei for a survey. It is reported that the location of the iron bridge is 35 miles north of Pingyuan Station and 4 miles south of Yellow River Cliff Station. The Yellow River's old channel belongs to Lijiamiao. The place that was blown up is the eighth hole from north to south. The blown-off length is 25 meters, and two steel beams for installing sleepers are damaged. Because the steel beams are German goods, they still need to be purchased from Germany, and about 2,000 yuan is needed. If it is necessary to repair and resume traffic urgently, only sleepers can be used to support the roof first to lay railway tracks. It is estimated that 5,000 sleepers are needed. All available sleepers in Jinan have been collected, but it is still difficult to meet this number. Although there are many sleepers stored in Pukou, about 100,000, there are no vehicles and they cannot be transported. Therefore, there is currently no way. Engineer Hu has drawn a picture and submitted it to the Tianjin-Pukou Railway Bureau for review. (8th)

Zhang Huizan Appointed Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Jiangxi Province 76

A Nanchang dispatch from the 7th reports that bandit-communists in Jiangxi Province are rampant, ravaging over twenty counties, and have not been completely eradicated for a long time. It is now heard that General Commander Chiang Kai-shek has discussed suppression methods with Division Commanders Jin Handing and Zhang Huizan, and with Zhang's agreement, has appointed Zhang as the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Jiangxi Province. The 18th Division Headquarters received a telegram from the General Headquarters yesterday: "To the 18th Division Headquarters in Nanchang: Division Commander Zhang Huizan of the 18th Division is hereby appointed as Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Jiangxi Province. All troops stationed in Jiangxi Province shall be under his command. A separate telegram and commission order will be issued. You are to comply accordingly. [Signed] Zhong Zheng, [Stamped] Wei Can." It has just been learned from a telegram from Zhang in Beijing to Chief of Staff Xiao of the 18th Division that Zhang is scheduled to depart on the 5th to return to the province, inspecting the defenses of northern Jiangxi and the Nanxun Railway along the way. He should arrive in the province today or tomorrow. After Zhang arrives in the province, he will go to western Jiangxi to command the various brigades to eradicate Zhu De and Mao Zedong. As for the situation of the Jiangxi bandits, a report has just been received from Cheng Brigade in Ji'an that the main force of Zhu De has retreated to Donggu, at the junction of Xingguo, Yongfeng, Ningdu, and Ji'an. This is Zhu's old nest (when Zhu retreated from Fujian, Li Shaojiu and Duan Yuequan used this as their base). In the area of Pitou and Chikou, government troops are still pursuing them. The incoming telegram is recorded below: (1) According to a phone report from Regiment Commander Peng, the main force of Zhu De and Mao Zedong has now retreated to Donggu, Fukou, and Pitou. Only a few robbers are present in Zhangjiadu and Futan. Furthermore, the bandits who previously crossed the Yinxia River were defeated by Zeng Battalion and retreated to the east bank. (2) According to a phone call from Regiment Commander Huang, the Independent 23rd Regiment of the bandit army, which attacked Anfu County the day before yesterday, was defeated by the two battalions led by Zhi and Wen. The bandits then fled to Longzhou Xiaochikou. Wei has dispatched Guan Battalion, the Sanqutan Guerrilla Team led by Wang Mingde, and the Yongxin Peacekeeping Team led by Gu Chonghan to suppress them. Furthermore, a visitor from Jishui said that when Zhu's bandits attacked Jishui City, Tang Brigade firmly defended the city. Zhu De then led a large force to cross the river and besiege the city. Coincidentally, Zhu Brigade and Yi Regiment arrived and saw the bandits crossing the river in civilian boats, so they took the opportunity to attack. Gunfire and artillery shells rained down, sinking many bandit boats. About a thousand bandits were either hit by stray bullets or drowned. The siege of Jishui has now been lifted. The newly appointed County Magistrate Cheng Daozhou, because order has been restored in the county, took a boat to Jishui on the 6th to take office.

Taiwanese Ice Fish Flood Quanzhou 77

A Xiamen dispatch reports that most coastal residents in Fujian Province engage in fishing. Their methods still use old-fashioned nets, which require a lot of labor but yield little fish. Furthermore, they lack ice storage facilities, so the abundance of fish depends on the tides or the weather. The market often feels that supply cannot meet demand, or supply exceeds demand, resulting in the highest and lowest value fluctuations. Fishermen also feel that if they catch little, it is not enough to make a living, and if they catch a lot, they must sell it immediately. Last year, a Japanese fishing company planned to develop the South China Sea fishing grounds, which it later implemented, using machine trawlers to fish in the Taiwan Strait and between Fuzhou, Quanzhou, and Xiamen. Wherever the trawlers went, the fish schools were emptied. Our country's old-style manual fishing cannot compete. As a result, the coastal fishing industry has been greatly affected. The Japanese fishing company is very large. After catching fish, it immediately places them in ice storage ships, carries them back to Taiwan, stores them in ice cellars, and then transports them to other ports for sale according to market needs. Last August, Quanzhou fish merchant Chen Longqing went to Taiwan by steamship to sell large quantities of frozen fresh fish in Quanzhou. The value was cheaper than that obtained by local methods, and there was an adequate supply of various types of fish. As a result, everyone bought Taiwanese ice fish. Recently, the Quanzhou market has been flooded with Taiwanese ice fish, and the local fishing industry is declining rapidly. According to people in the fishing industry, the losses to the domestic fishing industry in Quanzhou during the past six or seven months are no less than hundreds of thousands of yuan. This month, the Jinjiang fishermen felt that foreign aggression was increasing daily, and they had to seek resistance to survive. Kang Sirui and others promoted the organization of a fishing industry union to unite the fishermen of Quanzhou and Hui'an into a large-scale organization and to establish a cooperative to resist Japanese fish. It has been reported to the local party headquarters and the government for record. (March 6th)

The Arrogance of Russians in Manzhouli 78

Galloping Through the Streets, Singing and Shouting Late at Night

Forming Teams to Patrol and Transport Contraband

Beating Our Military Police and Lodging Protests

A Harbin dispatch from the 4th reports that at 10:40 PM on February 28th, two teams of Soviet infantry, about 300 officers and soldiers, 100 cavalrymen, and over 100 artillerymen and special forces, along with two aircraft, 13 automobiles, and armored vehicles, arrived on the main road from Dauri to Abagaitu on the Manchurian border. On the morning of March 1st, more infantry and cavalry arrived, and military transport vehicles continued to come and go. According to our investigation, there are already more than two regiments of Russian cavalry stationed in Abagaitu, with approximately one battalion each of artillery and infantry. This place is only a short distance from our border. What is the purpose? It is unknown. However, according to the Soviet international reception staff stationed in Manzhouli, it is because White Russian warfare was discovered in Sanhe within our territory, and heavy troops are stationed on the border to prevent the White Party. But this does not match the situation at the Russian consulate in Manzhouli. Because on the 26th of last month, 31 soldiers from the Russian State Defense Political Bureau, in several military vehicles, drove directly into Manzhouli Station and stopped in front of the Russian consulate. The vehicles were loaded with 68 huge boxes. Judging from the difficulty of moving them, it can be determined that they must contain military supplies. When Manzhouli Customs attempted to inspect, they were forcibly refused. In recent days, many young Russians have been entering and exiting the Russian consulate, all wearing plain clothes and carrying handguns, rampaging through the streets and causing trouble everywhere. Merchants and residents close their shops in succession after 5:00 PM. In the Tolan-nor area, Soviet Russian plainclothes propaganda teams have appeared, spreading leaflets and promoting communism in groups of three or five. The Chinese merchants in the coal mine area, who had gradually returned after the war, are now unable to live in peace and are panicking and fleeing to the interior. It is also rumored that Russian plainclothes soldiers are densely stationed around the Manzhouli area. Each Red Russian worker at each station has received handguns and bombs. If the Sino-Russian official conference can see the dawn, there may be no trouble on the border. Otherwise, once it breaks down, a major chaos could erupt at any moment. As for the ferocity and disorder of the Russian Red Party in Manzhouli Station, it is beyond the control of the police force. One day, at 11:30 PM, three policemen from the Russian consulate clashed with a special police patrol leader named Shang at the corner of Wudao Street in Manzhouli Station because they did not know the password and broke through the sentry post. The three Russian policemen actually snatched Shang's handgun. At around 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 2nd, more than 30 members of the Red Party galloped through the streets, with bare arms, singing loudly, causing pedestrians to avoid them. When passing Erdao Street, they encountered Chen Zhende, a soldier from the Sixth Company of the 51st Regiment under Liang Zhongjia. The Russians called together workers from the electric light factory and over 100 members of the youth party and surrounded Chen, attacking him. Over ten special police officers, including Liu Baoxin, Zhao Delong, and road patrolman Ren Fayou, arrived to mediate and were also beaten, and Liu Baoxin's handgun was taken. Later, a large team of military police came to rescue Chen Zhende and sent him to the hospital for treatment. He was seriously injured. The military police then arrested five Red Party members who committed the crime and sent them to the police station. In the evening, the Russian side protested and demanded the release of the people from the police station. Shao Qinghuai, the chief of the Third Special Police Headquarters, came to Harbin today to request instructions. The arrogance of the Russians is becoming increasingly evident.

Hangzhou Fast Mail 79

Because of financial constraints, Governor Zhang Jingjiang of the Provincial Government is urgently seeking solutions, and the construction expenses to be paid are very large. Today (the 10th) at 9:00 PM, a banquet was held at the Laiyin Xiaozhu on West Lake (Zhang's mansion) to discuss loan matters with Chairman Wang of the General Chamber of Commerce and over twenty people from the banking and money industries, including Jin Runquan and Mi Tingfang. Shen Ming and others, members of the Provincial Capital Three Granaries Committee, believe that the porridge factory at Qiyu is being extended by one month until the end of this month, and rice prices are soaring, making life difficult for the common people. They have decided to petition the Department of Civil Affairs to start selling grain at subsidized prices ahead of schedule. However, the current stock of 5,000 stones of grain is only enough for one month. It is proposed to request the Department of Civil Affairs to allocate 60,000 yuan of subsidized grain funds approved last year in order to rush to buy grain.

Qian Wenxuan, the director of the Liangzhe Audit Branch, went to Yushao Changchan on the 2nd of this month to inspect the production area and summoned the chiefs of the weighing and releasing bureau and the field magistrate to discuss measures to rectify production and sales and expand tax revenue. He then went from Yao to Ningbo and Shanghai to present the proposed rectification measures to Chief Supervisor Zhu of the Audit General Office for review. He returned to Hangzhou yesterday. (March 10th)

Local Correspondence Suzhou 80

Military prisoners transferred to military prison. The military prisoners held in the Caohejing Jiangsu Second Prison have been transferred. Fifty prisoners were escorted by troops from the Garrison Command to Suzhou in January and transferred to the Second Army Prison. Yesterday (the 10th), a platoon of troops from the Garrison Command, led by Platoon Leader Qiu, arrived at the Caohejing Second Prison at 3:00 PM to pick up 100 military prisoners and escorted them to the Army Prison for detention.

The High Court will recruit prison staff. Lin, the president of the Jiangsu High Court, recently investigated the escape of prisoners from county detention centers. This is due to the poor management of the prison staff. Although there have been frequent transfers, there is a lack of competent personnel. Therefore, he specially petitioned the Ministry of Justice to formulate regulations to recruit prison staff. Once the Ministry approves the order, the recruitment will begin and personnel will be dispatched to various detention centers to take office. Counter-revolutionary prisoners from Taixian are escorted to Suzhou. The Taixian County Government in northern Jiangsu (the 10th) ordered the county police to escort four counter-revolutionary prisoners, Zhou Rongcai, Zhou Rongde, Tang Changhe, and Gao Qibao, to Suzhou to be sent to the High Court for review.

A major theft case. The residence of a Shanxi man named Yao, located at No. 24 Miaotang in Xumen, was robbed at 3:00 PM on the 7th of this month. Jewelry, antiques, and 140 yuan in silver dollars, 360 yuan in banknotes were stolen, totaling about 2,000 yuan in losses. The housewife reported the theft to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation. The thief was spotted buying a bicycle on the road outside Changmen the evening before last (the 9th) by Detective Team Leader Zhou Hongjiang, who arrested him. According to his confession, he is named Wang Sanbao and is a disciple of the notorious rogue Xu Gengsheng. Team Leader Zhou accompanied him to the Zhaoshang Hotel, found the stolen goods, and took them all to the bureau for transfer to the local court for review.

Actively collecting exhibits from eight counties. The municipal and county governments and the General Chamber of Commerce, in preparation for participating in the Wuxi Eight County and City Product Exhibition, held a meeting at the General Chamber of Commerce yesterday (the 10th) and decided to jointly organize a collection of exhibits. The address is temporarily at the General Chamber of Commerce, and the expenses are shared equally. April 5th is the deadline for collection, and the review will be held for five days. On the 10th, the exhibits will be sent to Wuxi for display. The collection office plans to appoint three committee members: Xu Woyun from the municipal government, Wu Zhuxi from the Chamber of Commerce, and the county government has not yet determined.

Social Daily reporter released on bail. The Suzhou Social Daily, due to careless reporting, was ordered to be suspended by Regiment Commander Xu of the stationed army, and the editor-in-chief Lu Yiran was arrested. It has been many days now. Lu Yiran was released on bail at noon yesterday (the 10th). Whether the newspaper can be published as usual is still subject to review by higher authorities.

Songjiang 81

Minutes of the County Government Meeting. The County Government held its 48th County Government Meeting the day before yesterday to discuss the following matters: (1) The District Chief of the 12th District reported that no one is responsible for erecting the grain map foundation in the fifth area. It was decided that land registration is currently being implemented, and the County Magistrate should order the District Chief to supervise the investigation of farmland owed by households. If there are any who conceal their land and do not pay taxes, they should be reported to the government for approval to confiscate the land for relief. (2) The District Chief of the 12th District reported that the land in the fifth area is mixed with county fields, and the people are evading tax payment. It was requested that the Construction Bureau should be instructed to jointly survey the salt fields. It was decided that the case is related to land survey and should be submitted to the Land Consolidation Committee for review. (3) How to crack down on rickshaw pullers who do not comply with the price list set by the Construction Bureau. It was decided that the County Magistrate should instruct the Public Security Bureau to instruct the Second District Branch to set up a post at the railway station to strictly crack down on offenders. Those who violate the regulations will be detained and investigated, and the Construction Bureau will strictly formulate measures and issue a notice. (4) The First and Second Districts jointly requested the allocation of funds for dredging the river to dredge Guanshaotang Maojing. It was decided that the County Magistrate should instruct the Property Department to allocate funds.

Standing Committee of the Property Department. The County Property Management Office held a standing committee meeting on the 10th. Zhang Xiaomei presided over the meeting. The agenda included the repair of the Confucian Temple and the allocation of funds for dredging the river. There were resolutions to reply to the County Government. It was also learned that the office staff unanimously submitted their resignations due to the expiration of their terms of office. For the accumulated grain funds, it was decided to transfer them to the Accumulated Grain Management Committee for safekeeping. However, the term of the office has two months left.

Verdict in an extortion case. The case of Wu Bogeng, a gentry in the town, who received a threatening letter last winter demanding a large sum of money, was investigated by the Public Security Bureau after Wu reported it. Yin Bohua, a patrol officer from the First District Branch, arrested two suspicious men and women, including Shen Shiqing, in a certain place. Because that place was the agreed place for the extortion and it was a place that Shen and others did not usually go to, their actions were very suspicious. After being arrested and sent to the county, they were interrogated repeatedly. The case was proposed and sentenced today. Shen Shiqing was sentenced to two months in prison, and his wife was released on bail.

A woman lost her gold bracelet on her way to Shanghai. Yesterday (the 10th), a mother and daughter named Li and a maid from outside the West Gate of Songjiang planned to take the 1:09 PM express train to Shanghai. When the train arrived at Songjiang Station, it was extremely crowded. After the three of them boarded the train one after another, Mrs. Li took money out of her cheongsam pocket to give to the porters. Unexpectedly, a gold bracelet (weighing about nine qian and five fen) and forty yuan in banknotes wrapped in silk were exposed and stolen by a pickpocket. When Mrs. Li was seated, the train had already started, and she realized what had happened. She immediately called the train police to investigate, but there was no trace. However, according to Mrs. Li, when I sat down, it seemed to be still by my side, so a certain young man next to me was highly suspected. Later, when the train arrived at Shanghai Station, after inspection, nothing was found. It seems that the fate of losing money cannot be reversed. It is heard that Mrs. Li is the sister of Li Zuchun. This trip to Shanghai is for her son to marry someone in Shanghai.

Jiading 82

Lu Shen was falsely accused and detained. Lu Linzhu, the director of the County Public Education Center, was walking home from the center at about 5:00 PM on the 8th when he was arrested by the Public Security Bureau detective team and sent to the County Government. For a time, the reason was unknown, and the people were shocked. Jin Boqin from the Chamber of Commerce and Lu Shunxiang from the Education Association, along with seven or eight others, visited County Magistrate Chen to inquire about the truth and request bail. It was then learned that it was a secret order from the Department of Civil Affairs to arrest and monitor the case. The reason was that Zhuge Zhongwen, who lived in the eastern township of this county, had mailed a report to the Department of Civil Affairs accusing Lu Linxun, Shen Zhongxuan, the head of Lianxi Elementary School, Pan Zhijiu, the director of academic affairs, Ji Hanjun, Zhang Naizhang, Zhang Changjiao, the former county executive committee members, and Yu Guanli and Xia Menghuan, the workers, of having solid evidence of reaction. After visiting the people involved, investigating the evidence, it was all false. Moreover, no one named Zhuge has been heard of in the entire county. It is obviously a false accusation. They immediately requested bail, but it was not allowed. At about 3:00 AM that night, Shen Zhongxuan was also arrested by detectives in Nanxiang and sent to Jiading to be detained in the police team with Lu. The people in the education community were greatly dissatisfied when they heard the news and went to the Education Bureau to ask Director Yang to negotiate with the county and meet with the county magistrate. As a result, Lu and Shen were temporarily released on bail.

A theft occurred in Qian Mingtang. The villagers of Qian Mingtang, west of Li, Ding Ruixing and Shen Rongchang, had some savings. On the evening of the 9th, more than ten thieves suddenly came, broke open the gate, and searched wantonly. Failing to get what they wanted, they used fire to burn the fingers of Ding's wife to force her to reveal where the gold was hidden. They escaped after a while.

The rice industry is holding subsidized sales. Recently, the price of rice in Kunyi has risen to more than 16 yuan per stone. It is difficult for the poor people to get enough to eat. The Rice Industry Association has sent special personnel to Shanghai to purchase a large amount of indica rice to Kunshan to hold subsidized sales to benefit the poor. It is scheduled to be sold at the Rice Industry Association in the Zhou Ting Alley of Jishi on the 15th, at a price of 1.5 jiao of ocean per liter.

The meeting to restore firefighting was fruitless. District Chief Yan Huating of the First District said that since the city's fire brigades had clashed with the Public Security Bureau inspectors during a fire the day before yesterday, and eight people had been detained, all the members of the district fire brigades had resigned, resulting in no one to put out the fire when a fire broke out. Therefore, at 1:00 PM on the 9th, the First District Office, together with the County Party Headquarters and the County Chamber of Commerce, invited the executive committee members of the Firefighting Federation and the directors of each district and member representatives to hold a joint meeting in the District Office to discuss how to restore firefighting. It adjourned at 6:00 PM without result.

The battalion commander arrested counter-revolutionaries. Liang Battalion Commander immediately led soldiers to investigate and arrest them. They arrested three counter-revolutionaries, including Qin Linjiang, a ferocious woman, in the hotel and took them back to the battalion headquarters for detention, pending report to the regimental headquarters for review. Zhang Guobiao and Nong Decai, the platoon leaders of the battalion, also received a report from their soldiers at 8:00 AM yesterday, stating that the communist Liu A'er was plotting wrongdoing and was now hiding in a grass shed at the foot of Yinglong Bridge outside the West Gate. Zhang and Nong immediately went to the West Gate to cooperate with Wang Hongshan, the patrolman of the Fourth Branch of the Public Security Bureau in charge of the area, to arrest them. Liu A'er was arrested, and two suspects, Yang Changqing and Xu Yang, were also arrested. Several counter-revolutionary slogans were found in Xu's home. They were immediately taken to the bureau and temporarily detained pending review.

The director of the detention center took office. Chen Fengya, the director of the county government detention center, was recently transferred by the High Court to serve as a prison staff member and director of the detention center in Yangzhong County. Wang Nianci, the director of the Fengxian County detention center, was transferred to Xizheng to take over the vacant position. Mr. Wang came to Xizheng to take office the day before yesterday.

Thorough investigation of the case of being swindled at the Western Tobacco Shop. Tongcheng Xiehecheng Western Tobacco Shop was suddenly searched for two hours by armed policemen sent by the County Public Security Bureau without finding anything. Then Zhao Dongchen, the manager of the shop, paid 250 yuan to settle the matter. The incident was widely publicized. When the County Office learned of it, County Magistrate Chen immediately summoned the manager of the shop to inquire about the facts. Zhao has submitted a supplementary statement requesting a thorough investigation, which is attracting much attention from all walks of life.

A fierce battle with bandits in Jinsha. More than 100 bandits suddenly arrived in Jinlong Township, Jinsha, and committed robbery. After the police team and the defense corps fought back, a fierce battle lasted for two hours. The police and the corps retreated due to running out of ammunition. Fortunately, the main force came to support, and the bandits began to retreat.

Jiangyin 88

Hua Mingbao was strangled to death. Hua Mingbao, a resident of Huaxue Village, Sanguanpailoutou, Second District, used to be a policeman. He was suddenly strangled to death with a rope the night before last and suffered knife wounds. A snail picker saw it in the river and reported it to his family. The cause of his death is unknown.

Qian Shouming received a threatening letter. Qian Yixiang (managed by Liyong), a wealthy businessman in Qingguo Alley, held a funeral on the 10th and a family sacrifice on the 9th, which was extremely grand. Earlier, his son Shouming suddenly received a threatening letter signed Chen Jian, a certain minister, demanding 2,000 yuan and setting a deadline for payment. The Qian family has no solution after receiving the letter.

Li Xinqi was shot dead by bandits. The family of Li Xinqi, a resident of Huaxi Sanduan, Ninth District, Weizhengzhuzhuang, has three brothers and a small but well-off family business. At about 10:00 PM the night before last (the 7th), more than twenty thieves went to rob them. The Li family had several courtyards, and they broke in layer by layer. Xinqi confronted the thieves and was shot several times by the thieves. Three bullets hit his vital parts and he died on the spot. The family suffered only minor losses. The thieves went to Zhouzhuang. Today (the 9th), Prosecutor Tong Chen went to the countryside to inspect. Also, the home of Zhu Yinlin in Songfengtou, Mazhen, Fourteenth District, was robbed by more than ten bandits the night before last. The hospital established a large-scale arrest of smokers. After the establishment of the County Anti-Smoking Hospital, very few people went to quit. Zhenjiang 89

Danish Crown Prince Visits Province Today: Danish Crown Prince Frederik, along with his brother and the Crown Princess of Denmark, a party of seven, arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday. They plan to take the opportunity of traveling to Beijing on the 12th to visit the scenic spots of Jinshan and Jiaoshan in our province. Chairman Lu of the local Chamber of Commerce received a telegram from a friend in Shanghai yesterday, stating that the Danish Crown Prince, etc., will be traveling to our province on the Hai Rong warship today. It is reported that the Danish Crown Prince's visit to Zhenjiang is purely for sightseeing and they decline any local official receptions. Preparation for the Local Products Exhibition of Eight Counties: Sun Zuji, the Magistrate of Wuxi County, considers Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, Jiangyin, Yixing, Changshu, etc., to be prosperous industrial and commercial areas of Jiangsu Province. He plans to organize a local products exhibition of eight counties in Huishan Town to promote local industry. He has drafted regulations and submitted them to the Provincial Government to be forwarded to the Ministry of Interior for approval.

Recent Rice Prices Continue to Rise: Zhenjiang rice prices have been gradually increasing due to the shortage of supply caused by the disasters in Jiangbei. Recently, continuous rainfall has further reduced supply from the countryside around Heshia, causing market prices to rise by another four or five jiao per shi (unit of dry measure) compared to the previous two days. Yesterday, the selling price of foreign xiān rice had risen to 18.3 yuan per shi, while the price of "Ri Tang" rice was 17 yuan per shi, the second grade was 16.7 yuan per shi, and even ordinary rice was priced at 16.2 yuan per shi. According to people in the trade, if there is no large-scale supply to alleviate the situation in the short term, not only is there no hope of price reduction, but prices are expected to continue to rise.

Arrest of Bandit Leader Cai Hanyu: Cai Hanyu, the bandit leader who captured Liyang in November last year, was arrested at the Japanese-owned Songjia Hotel in Zhabei, Shanghai, at 7:30 PM on the 7th. The arresting officer was Chen, the squad leader of the water patrol team from Wu County. Cai Hanyu confessed that he was appointed Jiangyin Commander by the Reorganization Faction and admitted to leading the attack on Liyang. He was handed over to the Special Municipal Public Security Bureau. Yesterday (the 10th),

Zhao Yuecheng and other detectives from the Provincial Public Security Bureau, dispatched by the Department of Civil Affairs, went to Shanghai to escort Cai Hanyu back. They passed through Suzhou after 4 PM. The Wu County Public Security Bureau specially dispatched detectives Li Yongfu, Mao Shouyu, Zhu Jinlian, and Su Yuting to accompany the escort to Zhenjiang. The bandit was subject to a reward of 5,000 yuan issued by the Department of Civil Affairs for his capture. It is confirmed that he is Cai Laowu. The reports in Shanghai newspapers these days about the Taihu bandit leader robbing Puzhuang, etc., are not true. These were pretexts used by the investigating detectives because the bandit had a great influence in Shanghai with many followers, and they dared not reveal the arrest easily before escorting him back to Zhenjiang for fear of accidents.

Yangzhou 90

Robbery Next to the Bus Station: Last night (the 8th), at midnight, eight or nine bandits suddenly broke into the house of Zong Kuanfu outside Fuyun Gate, west of the bus station, to rob. However, they mistakenly entered the house of Kuanfu's cousin, Kuanhong. A night watchman noticed the front door of the Zong residence was wide open, and knew something was wrong. He started banging his gong wildly. Neighbors were awakened from their dreams and came out. The bandits, seeing the situation was not good, only stole clothing and accessories worth over a hundred yuan and fled. Request to Dredge River Channels: The Fifth District Office of Jiangdu received a letter from villagers such as Huan Jiazhen, stating that there have been many droughts in recent years, and the river water is shallow, leading to poor harvests. They requested that the river channels be dredged to facilitate irrigation. The district office gathered nearby residents to dredge the channels manually, starting from the Xiasha River Estuary to the north end of the Huanjia Lane, a length of over 2,000 zhang (unit of measure), requiring approximately 4,000 labor days. Households with land would provide labor based on acreage. The district chief has submitted the letter to the county government for review.

Meeting to Distribute Relief Funds: The Jiangdu County Government, because the Jiangdu Relief Association had received relief funds from the province, will hold a meeting on March 12 to discuss how much county funds have been raised and how to distribute them.

Qingjiang 91

Police Arrest Reactionary Criminals: Shao Zhen, the Second Squad Leader of the Third Company of the Huaiyin Police Team, along with Zhang Yuzhen, the Captain of the Special Police Team of the Public Security Bureau, were ordered to go to Zhuji Village, Tongxing Township, in the Third District to arrest Wu Shaotang, Li Buqing, and Wu Hongfei on the morning of the 6th. It is said that Wu Shaotang and Li Buqing were ordered by reactionary factions to create the Small Knife Society and the Divine Fist Red Spear Yellow Tassel Three Societies in the township. Wu was the commander of the five societies, and Li was the deputy commander. Wu Hongfei was responsible for assisting in the Knife Society. They forced people to join the society in the villages. Five charms and four charm belts of the Knife Society, seven broadswords, two rifles, one ox horn whistle, and two copper horns were found in Wu Shaotang's home. They were immediately escorted to the battalion headquarters and then to the county government for interrogation.

Fu Yun Steamer Robbed: The Changban steamer of the Fu Yun Company was traveling on the inland river on the night of the 4th when it arrived at Jiulong Bay in Sishui. Suddenly, seven bandits appeared, each holding a handgun or Mauser pistol, and ordered the steamer to stop. The sailors and drivers did not dare to resist and stopped the steamer immediately. The bandits jumped on board and searched at will, robbing over 20 yuan of silver from the waterman's cabin, three leather jackets from passengers, over 50 yuan of silver, and a gold ring.

Jiaxing 92

Large Number of Bandit Boats Discovered in Ma Port: The waterways in the northern countryside of Jiaxing are intricate, with many rivers and lakes, so robberies are frequent in the area. Last year, Ma Port and other places in the northern countryside were robbed multiple times, and people were kidnapped for ransom. Although the water police dispatched teams to investigate, the cases were difficult to solve. It is now reported that on the 9th, nineteen bandit boats suddenly arrived in Ma Port in the northern countryside (about three li from Dihui Town), with over two hundred bandits. They landed at the location, set up stoves to cook, and took turns standing guard and eating meals. After the meal, they all boarded the boats, untied them, and sailed to the Jiadian area further north, where they again landed and stood guard. In the afternoon at 4 PM, the Jiaxing Water Police District Headquarters heard the news and dispatched shallow-water warships to tow patrol boats to pursue and suppress the bandits.

Pay Attention to Preventing the Spread of Epidemics: The Jiaxing County Government, because the spread of meningitis inside and outside the city is already severe, ordered the Public Security Bureau yesterday that the families of those who die from epidemics must place the corpses in coffins and bury them on the same day. In order to prevent the spread of the disease, before the epidemic is completely eliminated, all boys and girls under the age of sixteen should be absolutely prohibited from entering amusement venues or theaters to avoid danger.

Pinghu 93

Speculation Failure Leads to Brother's Sacrifice: Chen Lianting, who lives outside the West Gate, is engaged in business in Xinjia, and his family is fairly well-off. His younger brother, Wuting, is engaged in business in Shanghai and has a wide circle of friends. Recently, due to the soaring gold prices, he failed in speculation, losing over 50,000 yuan and unable to make up for it. He returned to Pinghu last month to borrow money from his brother to try again. Unexpectedly, he failed again, overwhelmed with resentment, and hanged himself in Shanghai at the end of last month. Lianting received the news, thinking of the fraternal bond and the large sums of money lost, and in a fit of anger, drowned himself in the river the day before yesterday. It is truly tragic.

Hangzhou 94

Planning to Build the Qiantang River Bridge: The Zhejiang Construction Department considers the Qiantang River to be an important transportation route in eastern Zhejiang, and the Qiantang River Bridge needs to be built urgently. It is proposed to first establish a Qiantang River Bridge Engineering Design Committee. The organizational charter has already been revised and approved by the Provincial Government Conference. The department announced yesterday that Jiang Zundi, Chen Ticheng, Hong Jiayi, Hou Jiayuan, and Lu Fengshu have been appointed as members to prepare for the project. Discussions on Financial Relief: Zhejiang Province urgently needs large construction funds, about 5 million yuan, but the provincial treasury is empty. It is proposed to ask the Provincial Government to find ways to provide relief. It is reported that the department has rushed to complete the list of expenses and will submit it to the Provincial Government Conference today (the 11th) for discussion on solutions.

Immigration and Reclamation of Sanmen Bay: Zhejiang Province has decided to handle the case of immigration and reclamation of Sanmen Bay. It is reported that the Provincial Government has sent personnel to investigate the number of fields and immigrants. They will be handed over to the Northeast Immigration Committee for handling: (1) Liangtian 10,200 mu, requiring 1,800 immigrants; (2) Qinei Port 51,000 mu, requiring 5,400 immigrants; (3) Yuejing Port 26,000 mu, requiring 2,200 immigrants; (4) Bailiu Port 21,000 mu, requiring 1,500 immigrants.

Xiaoshan 95

Prohibition of Grain Export: The Xiaoshan County Executive Committee, in order to prevent the export of grain from the county, has drafted two prohibition measures: (1) All ships from Xixing to Shaoxing carrying more than 20 shi of rice must provide a guarantee to the local government; (2) The government will verify the guarantee and issue a passport before allowing export. The measures have been submitted to the Provincial Executive Committee, which will forward them to the Provincial Government for Xiaoshan County Government to implement.

No One Registers for Immigration to the Northeast: The Xiaoshan County Government previously received a telegram from the Department of Civil Affairs, stating that the deadline for reporting the number of people who have registered for immigration and reclamation is the end of March. The deadline is approaching. County Magistrate Du has gone to the countryside to promote the program, but the people of Xiaoshan have a deep-rooted attachment to their homeland. To date, no one has registered. Yesterday, County Magistrate Du reported the situation to the Department of Civil Affairs for review.
